 aane vaala 30 june kaa din aadhikarik rup se ek second lanbaa rahane vaala he, kyonki mangalvaar ko hamaara samay ek second ke liye ruk jayega
 That is, where there are usually 60 seconds in a minute, on June 30, the last minute of the day will be 61 seconds
 america antariksh vigyaan agency nasa ne isaki pushti kar di he
 Actually, there are 86,400 seconds in a day, but on June 30 this time will add an extra second i
e
 leap second
 nasake marilland ke greenbelt main godard spes flite centre ke danniel macmillan ke mutabik, 'prithvi kaa parikraman dhire-dhire dhimaa ho rahaa he isliye isamen atirikt lipsecondjud gaya he
 'this is according to Coordinated Universal Time i
e
 UTC, which people use in daily life
 utisi atomic time he, jahaan ek second kii avadhi sisium ke atoms main hone vaale purvanumanit electromagnetic transishan ke aadhaar par hoti he
 These transitions are so reliable that the cesium clock can last up to 1,400,000 years
 nasa nebayaan jari kar kaha, 'prithvi, chand or surya ke bich gurutvkarshan bal kii vajah se prithvi kaa ghurnan dhimaa ho rahaa he
 'why is being added UTC system was introduced on 1 January 1960 to reconcile leap second atomic and solar time
 1972 se hi jarurat padane par utisi main badlaav kar lip second joda ja rahaa he
 For this, an extra second is added at the last minute in June or December
 atirikt second jodne kaa kaam international arth roteshan and reference system sarvice ke dwaara kiya jaataa he
 In such a situation, time will be stopped for one second at the last minute of 30th June for synchronization of these two measurement values
 aisa hote hi aakhri minute 61 second kaa ho jayega
 What is leap year like? Under the rule of leap secondleep year an additional day is added to the calendar every four years
 aisa isliye kiya jaataa he kiprithviko surya ke chaaron ore chakkar lagane main 5 ghanta, 48 minute or 46 second kaa atirikt samay lagata he
 However, unlike leap time, no such calculation can be made when it will be added after a fixed period

 lekin apane desh kaa aadhaar card in sab cardon se behad alag he

 france se card kii shuruyatpahchaan patr kii parampara duniya main bahut puraani nahin he

 1803-04 main france aadhunik duniya kaa pehla aisa desh bana jisane apane nagarikon ke liye pahchaan patr kii shuruyaat kii

 aaj ke halaataj halaat hadal chuke hai or duniya kaaphi choti ho gai hai

 Political background: Farrukhabad Lok Sabha seat has been held nearly 15 times since Independence
 inamen se 7 baar congress ne jeet hasil kii he
 While three times BJP, twice SP, Janata Party twice and Janata Dal and United Socialist Party have won once
 aazaadee ke baad 1952 main hue loksabhaa chunaav main farrukhabad kaa ilaaka kanpur sansadeey seat ke tahat aata tha
 The elections to the Farrukhabad Lok Sabha were first contested in 1957 and Moolchand Dubey of the Congress won from here and reached the MP
